    14→export function useTeam(teamId: string | null): UseTeamResult {  
    15→  const [team, setTeam] = useState<Team | null>(null)  
    16→  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)  
    17→  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null)

    20→    if (!teamId) return

    22→      const res = await fetch(`/api/teams/${teamId}`)  
    23→      if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch team')

    26→      setError(null)  
    27→    } catch (err) {

    29→    }  
    30→  }, [teamId])

    30→  }, [teamId])  
    31→  
    32→  // Initial fetch  
    33→  useEffect(() => {  
    34→    if (!teamId) {  
    35→      setTeam(null)  
    36→      return  
    37→    }  
    38→    setLoading(true)  
    39→    fetchTeam().finally(() => setLoading(false))  
    40→  }, [teamId, fetchTeam])  
    41→  
    42→  const updateTeam = useCallback(async (updates: { name?: string; description?: string; agentIds?: string[]; instructions?: string }) => {  
    43→    if (!teamId) return  
    44→    // Optimistic update  
    45→    setTeam(prev => prev ? { ...prev, ...updates, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() } : prev)  
    46→    const res = await fetch(`/api/teams/${teamId}`, {  
    47→      method: 'PUT',  
    48→      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },  
    49→      body: JSON.stringify({ ...updates, lastActivityAt: new Date().toISOString() }),  
    50→    })  
    51→    if (!res.ok) {  
    52→      await fetchTeam() // Revert optimistic update  
    53→      throw new Error('Failed to update team')  
    54→    }  
    55→    const data = await res.json()  
    56→    setTeam(data.team)  
    57→  }, [teamId, fetchTeam])  
    58→  
    59→  return {  
    60→    team,  
    61→    loading,  
    62→    error,  
    63→    updateTeam,  
    64→    refreshTeam: fetchTeam,  
    65→  }  
    66→}

     2→ * Message Filter — enforces closed-team messaging isolation  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Determines whether a message from sender to recipient is allowed

Now I understand the logic. Looking at step 5 (lines 93-110): when a normal closed-team member sends a message, it checks if the recipient shares a team (line 95-99) or if the recipient is the COS of their team (line 102-105).

- Step 5, `canReachCOS`: checks if recipient is COS of any of sender's teams - COS-beta is NOT COS of team alpha, so false.  
- Result: denied.

   194→export function loadTeams(): Team[] {  
   195→  try {  
   196→    ensureTeamsDir()  
   197→    if (!fs.existsSync(TEAMS_FILE)) {  
   198→      return []  
   199→    }  
   200→    const data = fs.readFileSync(TEAMS_FILE, 'utf-8')  
   201→    const parsed: TeamsFile = JSON.parse(data)  
   202→    const teams = Array.isArray(parsed.teams) ? parsed.teams : []  
   203→  
   204→    // One-time idempotent migration: safe without lock because migration is append-only and convergent  
   205→    // Migration: ensure all teams have a type field (default to 'open')  
   206→    let needsSave = false  
   207→    for (const team of teams) {  
   208→      if (!team.type) {  
   209→        team.type = 'open'  
   210→        needsSave = true  
   211→      }  
   212→    }  
   213→    if (needsSave) {  
   214→      saveTeams(teams)  
   215→    }  
   216→  
   217→    return teams  
   218→  } catch (error) {  
   219→    console.error('Failed to load teams:', error)  
   220→    return []  
   221→  }  
   222→}  
   223→  
   224→export function saveTeams(teams: Team[]): boolean {  
   225→  try {  
   226→    ensureTeamsDir()  
   227→    const file: TeamsFile = { version: 1, teams }  
   228→    fs.writeFileSync(TEAMS_FILE, JSON.stringify(file, null, 2), 'utf-8')  
   229→    return true  
   230→  } catch (error) {  
   231→    console.error('Failed to save teams:', error)  
   232→    return false  
   233→  }  
   234→}

describe('verifyPassword', () => {
  it('returns true for correct password and false for wrong password', () => {
    /** Verifies password comparison against stored hash returns correct boolean */
    seedGovernance({ passwordHash: 'hashed:correctpass' })

    expect(verifyPassword('correctpass')).toBe(true)
    expect(verifyPassword('wrongpass')).toBe(false)
  })
})
```

**New:**  
```
describe('verifyPassword', () => {
  it('returns true for correct password and false for wrong password', () => {
    /** Verifies password comparison against stored hash returns correct boolean */
    seedGovernance({ passwordHash: 'hashed:correctpass' })

    expect(verifyPassword('correctpass')).toBe(true)
    expect(verifyPassword('wrongpass')).toBe(false)
  })

  it('returns false when no password has been set', () => {
    /** Verifies that verifyPassword returns false when passwordHash is null (no password configured) */
    seedGovernance({ passwordHash: null })

    expect(verifyPassword('anypassword')).toBe(false)
  })
})
```

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #FF9800; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

I can see the key difference: The GET handler checks `getTeam(id)` first and returns "Team not found" for non-existent teams. But the PUT and DELETE handlers do NOT check for team existence -- they go directly to `updateDocument` / `deleteDocument`, which will return null (document not found) rather than a specific "team not found" error. ## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-17 00:05:34]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #FF9800; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Now I have full understanding. The current behavior for PUT and DELETE on non-existent teams:  

- **PUT** on non-existent team: `updateDocument` loads docs for that team (returns `[]` since no file exists), can't find the docId, returns `null` -> route returns 404 with "Document not found" (NOT "Team not found")  
- **DELETE** on non-existent team: `deleteDocument` loads docs for that team (returns `[]`), filter doesn't remove anything, returns `false` -> route returns 404 with "Document not found" (NOT "Team not found")  

This is notable because the GET single-document endpoint DOES check for team existence first and returns "Team not found", but PUT and DELETE skip that check. I'll now add tests documenting this behavior.  

</div>


## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-17 00:05:40]*

```
describe('PUT /api/teams/[id]/documents/[docId]', () => {
  it('returns 404 when document does not exist', async () => {
    const req = makeRequest('/api/teams/team-1/documents/non-existent', {
      method: 'PUT',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ title: 'Updated' }),
    })
    const res = await updateDocumentRoute(req, makeParams('team-1', 'non-existent') as any)

    expect(res.status).toBe(404)
  })
```

**New:**  
```
describe('PUT /api/teams/[id]/documents/[docId]', () => {
  it('returns 404 when document does not exist', async () => {
    const req = makeRequest('/api/teams/team-1/documents/non-existent', {
      method: 'PUT',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ title: 'Updated' }),
    })
    const res = await updateDocumentRoute(req, makeParams('team-1', 'non-existent') as any)

    expect(res.status).toBe(404)
  })

  it('returns 404 with "Document not found" when team does not exist', async () => {
    /** PUT does not check team existence; it delegates to updateDocument which
     *  loads an empty doc list for the non-existent team and fails to find the docId. */
    const req = makeRequest('/api/teams/non-existent-team/documents/any-doc-id', {
      method: 'PUT',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ title: 'Updated' }),
    })
    const res = await updateDocumentRoute(req, makeParams('non-existent-team', 'any-doc-id') as any)

    expect(res.status).toBe(404)
    const data = await res.json()
    expect(data.error).toBe('Document not found')
  })
```

     1→/**  
     2→ * Message Filter — enforces closed-team messaging isolation  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Determines whether a message from sender to recipient is allowed  
     5→ * based on governance roles (MANAGER, Chief-of-Staff) and closed-team  
     6→ * membership. Open-world agents (not in any closed team) can message  
     7→ * freely unless the recipient is inside a closed team.  
     8→ */  
     9→  
    10→import { loadGovernance } from './governance'  
    11→import { loadTeams } from './team-registry'  
    12→  
    13→export interface MessageFilterInput {  
    14→  senderAgentId: string | null // null = mesh-forwarded message  
    15→  recipientAgentId: string  
    16→}  
    17→  
    18→export interface MessageFilterResult {  
    19→  allowed: boolean  
    20→  reason?: string  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→/**  
    24→ * Check whether a message from sender to recipient is allowed.  
    25→ *  
    26→ * Algorithm (R6.1–R6.7):  
    27→ * 1. Mesh-forwarded (senderAgentId null): always allowed (trust mesh peers)  
    28→ * 2. Neither in a closed team: allowed (open world, current behavior) (R6.4)  
    29→ * 3. Sender is MANAGER: always allowed (R6.3)  
    30→ * 4. Sender is COS of any closed team: can reach MANAGER, other COS, own team members (R6.2)  
    31→ * 5. Normal closed-team member: can reach same-team members and own COS (R6.1)  
    32→ * 6. Outside sender to closed-team recipient: denied (R6.5)  
    33→ * 7. Default: allowed  
    34→ *  
    35→ * IMPORTANT (R6.7): Uses getClosedTeamsForAgent (plural) to correctly handle  
    36→ * COS agents who belong to multiple closed teams simultaneously.  
    37→ */  
    38→export function checkMessageAllowed(input: MessageFilterInput): MessageFilterResult {  
    39→  const { senderAgentId, recipientAgentId } = input  
    40→  
    41→  // Step 1: Mesh-forwarded messages are always trusted  
    42→  if (senderAgentId === null) {  
    43→    return { allowed: true }  
    44→  }  
    45→  
    46→  // Single snapshot of all state — avoids redundant file reads from

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { loadGovernance, setPassword, verifyPassword } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→  
     4→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     5→  try {  
     6→    const body = await request.json()  
     7→    const { password, currentPassword } = body  
     8→  
     9→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string' || password.length < 6) {  
    10→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }, { status: 400 })  
    11→    }  
    12→  
    13→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    14→  
    15→    // If password already set, require current password  
    16→    if (config.passwordHash) {  
    17→      if (!currentPassword || !verifyPassword(currentPassword)) {  
    18→        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid current password' }, { status: 401 })  
    19→      }  
    20→    }  
    21→  
    22→    const isChange = !!config.passwordHash  
    23→    await setPassword(password)  
    24→  
    25→    if (isChange) {  
    26→      console.log('[governance] Password changed at', new Date().toISOString())  
    27→    } else {  
    28→      console.log('[governance] Password set at', new Date().toISOString())  
    29→    }  
    30→  
    31→    return NextResponse.json({ success: true })  
    32→  } catch (error) {  
    33→    console.error('Failed to set password:', error)  
    34→    return NextResponse.json(  
    35→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to set password' },  
    36→      { status: 500 }  
    37→    )  
    38→  }  
    39→}  
    40→

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { checkMessageAllowed } from '@/lib/message-filter'  
     3→import { loadAgents } from '@/lib/agent-registry'  
     4→  
     5→// In-memory cache: avoids re-reading governance + teams files for every agent  
     6→// on each request. TTL of 5 seconds balances freshness with performance.  
     7→const cache = new Map<string, { ids: string[]; expiresAt: number }>()  
     8→const CACHE_TTL_MS = 5_000  
     9→  
    10→export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {  
    11→  try {  
    12→    const agentId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('agentId')  
    13→  
    14→    if (!agentId) {  
    15→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId query parameter is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    16→    }  
    17→  
    18→    // Check cache first  
    19→    const cached = cache.get(agentId)  
    20→    if (cached && Date.now() < cached.expiresAt) {  
    21→      return NextResponse.json({ reachableAgentIds: cached.ids })  
    22→    }  
    23→  
    24→    // Cache miss or expired — compute reachable agents  
    25→    const allAgents = loadAgents()  
    26→    const reachableAgentIds: string[] = []  
    27→  
    28→    for (const agent of allAgents) {  
    29→      if (agent.id === agentId) continue  
    30→      if (agent.deletedAt) continue  
    31→  
    32→      const result = checkMessageAllowed({  
    33→        senderAgentId: agentId,  
    34→        recipientAgentId: agent.id,  
    35→      })  
    36→  
    37→      if (result.allowed) {  
    38→        reachableAgentIds.push(agent.id)  
    39→      }  
    40→    }  
    41→  
    42→    // Store in cache with TTL  
    43→    cache.set(agentId, { ids: reachableAgentIds, expiresAt: Date.now() + CACHE_TTL_MS })  
    44→  
    45→    // Evict stale/expired entries on every cache write to prevent unbounded growth  
    46→    const now = Date.now()  
    47→    for (const [key, entry] of cache) {  
    48→      if (now >= entry.expiresAt) cache.delete(key)  
    49→    }  
    50→  
    51→    r  

... [259 more chars truncated]

   303→export async function deleteTeam(id: string): Promise<boolean> {  
   304→  return withLock('teams', () => {  
   305→    const teams = loadTeams()  
   306→    const filtered = teams.filter(t => t.id !== id)  
   307→    if (filtered.length === teams.length) return false

   313→  })

     1→#!/bin/bash  
     2→# AI Maestro - Version Bump Script  
     3→# Centralizes version management across all files  
     4→#  
     5→# Usage:  
     6→#   ./scripts/bump-version.sh patch    # 0.17.12 -> 0.17.13  
     7→#   ./scripts/bump-version.sh minor    # 0.17.12 -> 0.18.0  
     8→#   ./scripts/bump-version.sh major    # 0.17.12 -> 1.0.0  
     9→#   ./scripts/bump-version.sh 0.18.0   # Set specific version

    42→        ;;  
    43→    minor)  
    44→        MINOR=$((MINOR + 1))  
    45→        PATCH=0  
    46→        NEW_VERSION="${MAJOR}.${MINOR}.${PATCH}"  
    47→        ;;  
    48→    major)  
    49→        MAJOR=$((MAJOR + 1))  
    50→        MINOR=0  
    51→        PATCH=0  
    52→        NEW_VERSION="${MAJOR}.${MINOR}.${PATCH}"  
    53→        ;;  
    54→    "")  
    55→        echo ""  
    56→        echo "Usage: $0 <patch|minor|major|version>"  
    57→        echo ""

   200→    async (teamId: string, targetAgentId: string): Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }> => {  
   201→      try {  
   202→        // Fetch current team to get existing agentIds  
   203→        const teamRes = await fetch(`/api/teams/${teamId}`)  
   204→        if (!teamRes.ok) return { success: false, error: 'Failed to fetch team' }  
   205→        const teamData = await teamRes.json()  
   206→        const team: Team = teamData.team  
   207→  
   208→        // Client-side COS removal guard (R4.7) — cannot remove COS from agentIds, server enforces too  
   209→        if (team.chiefOfStaffId === targetAgentId) {  
   210→          return { success: false, error: 'Cannot remove the Chief-of-Staff from team members — remove the COS role first' }  
   211→        }  
   212→

   219→        })

   222→        refresh()  
   223→        return { success: true }  
   224→      } catch (err) {  
   225→        return { success: false, error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to remove agent from team' }

    39→    // Acquire teams lock for the entire read-validate-write cycle to prevent TOCTOU races.

    90→  
    91→/** Resolve (approve or reject) a transfer request */  
    92→export async function resolveTransferRequest(  
    93→  id: string,  
    94→  status: 'approved' | 'rejected',  
    95→  resolvedBy: string,  
    96→  rejectReason?: string  
    97→): Promise<TransferRequest | null> {  
    98→  return withLock('transfers', () => {  
    99→    const requests = loadTransfers()  
   100→    const idx = requests.findIndex(r => r.id === id)  
   101→    if (idx === -1) return null  
   102→    if (requests[idx].status !== 'pending') return null // Already resolved  
   103→  
   104→    requests[idx] = {  
   105→      ...requests[idx],  
   106→      status,  
   107→      resolvedAt: new Date().toISOString(),  
   108→      resolvedBy,  
   109→      rejectReason: status === 'rejected' ? rejectReason : undefined,  
   110→    }  
   111→    saveTransfers(requests)  
   112→    return requests[idx]  
   113→  })  
   114→}  
   115→  
   116→// Exported for future scheduled cleanup integration  
   117→/** Clean up old resolved requests (older than 30 days) */

   123→    const cutoffStr = cutoff.toISOString()
